 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh on Friday attacked the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) for continuously stalling Parliament, saying that what happened in the monsoon session was a completely negative aspect of democracy
 unhone sahi soch rakhane vaale sabhi logon se apil kii ki ve uth khadey hon or bhaajapa se kahen ki vah loktantric sansthaaon main kaamkaaj chalane de
 Speaking to reporters in Parliament House Complex after the adjournment of the Parliament indefinitely, the Prime Minister said, "we should be proud that we have a functioning democracy
" lekin is satr main hamane jo kuch dekha, vah puri tarah iskaa nakaaratmak pahalu he
 "he told reporters," All right-thinking people in this country should stand up and jointly raise the voice that the parliamentary institutions should be allowed to function in accordance with the rules, which we are i only know " The monsoon session of Parliament was postponed indefinitely on Friday after a month

 4

 5

 6

 7

 Power is supplied to all coaches from these diesel generator bogies
 ise 'and on janareshan' (ioji) praudyogiki ke taur par janaa jaataa he
 Officials said that soon the department is going to start using 'head on Generation' (HOG) technology prevalent across the world
 is praudyogiki main railgadee ke upar se jane vaali bijli taron se hi dibbon ke liye bhi bijli lee jaati he
 Officials said that from October 2019, about 5,000 coaches of the Indian Railways will start operating with HOG technology
 isse trainon se janarator bogiyon ko hataane main madad milegi or unamem atirikt dibbe lagane kii sahuuliyat bhi milegi
 Not only this, the Railways will save more than Rs 6,000 crore annually on fuel
 sirf ek gaiyr-vaataanukoolit dibbe ko bijli aapurti karne ke liye prati ghanta 120 unit bijli kii jarurat hoti he
 The generator consumes 40 liters of diesel per hour to generate so much electricity
 vahiin vaataanukoolit dibbe ke liye eendhan kaa yahi khapat badhkar 65 se 70 litre dijal prati ghanta ho jaati he
 Officials said that the new system is environment friendly
 isamen vaayu or dhwani pradooshan nahin hoga
 It will also reduce carbon emissions by 700 tons per train per year
